            ];
            
            const brandSelect = document.getElementById("brand");
            const modelSelect = document.getElementById("model");
            const yearSelect = document.getElementById("year");
            const radiusSelect = document.getElementById("radius");
            const resultsDiv = document.getElementById("results");
            
            const brands = [...new Set(autoData.map(a => a.brand))];
            brands.forEach(brand => brandSelect.add(new Option(brand, brand)));
            
            brandSelect.addEventListener("change", function () {
                modelSelect.innerHTML = "<option value=''>Выберите модель</option>";
                yearSelect.innerHTML = "<option value=''>Выберите год</option>";
                radiusSelect.innerHTML = "<option value=''>Выберите радиус</option>";
                let models = autoData.filter(a => a.brand === this.value).map(a => a.model);
                [...new Set(models)].forEach(model => modelSelect.add(new Option(model, model)));
            });
            
            modelSelect.addEventListener("change", function () {
                yearSelect.innerHTML = "<option value=''>Выберите год</option>";
                radiusSelect.innerHTML = "<option value=''>Выберите радиус</option>";
                let years = autoData.filter(a => a.brand === brandSelect.value && a.model === this.value).map(a => a.year);
                [...new Set(years)].forEach(year => yearSelect.add(new Option(year, year)));
            });
            
            yearSelect.addEventListener("change", function () {
                radiusSelect.innerHTML = "<option value=''>Выберите радиус</option>";
                let selectedAuto = autoData.find(a => a.brand === brandSelect.value && a.model === modelSelect.value && a.year === this.value);
                if (!selectedAuto) return;
                selectedAuto.radius.forEach(r => radiusSelect.add(new Option(`R${r}`, r)));
            });
            
            radiusSelect.addEventListener("change", function () {
                resultsDiv.innerHTML = "";
                let selectedAuto = autoData.find(a => a.brand === brandSelect.value && a.model === modelSelect.value && a.year === yearSelect.value);
                if (!selectedAuto) return;
                
                let matchedDiscs = discsData.filter(d => d.pcd === selectedAuto.pcd && d.dia === selectedAuto.dia && d.radius == this.value);
                
                if (matchedDiscs.length > 0) {
                    matchedDiscs.forEach(disc => {
                        resultsDiv.innerHTML += `
                            <div>
                                <a href="${disc.url}" target="_blank">
                                    <img src="${disc.image}" alt="${disc.name}">
                                    <p>${disc.name} (Артикул: ${disc.article})</p>
                                </a>
                            </div>`;
                    });
                } else {
                    resultsDiv.innerHTML = "<p>Нет подходящих дисков</p>";
                }
            });
        });
    </script>
</head>

    <label for="radius">Радиус:</label>
    <select id="radius"><option value="">Выберите радиус</option></select>

    <div id="results"></div>
